TUR_minority_revolt_effect = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = TUR
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					resistance > 79.9
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { resistance > 79.9 }
				controller = { country_event = ottoman.0 }
			}
		}
	}
}

TUR_reduce_armenian_level = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level < 2 } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian = -0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian
			min = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian = -0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian
			min = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { state = 352 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.101 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 806 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.103 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 1022 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.134 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 881 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.135 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 355 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.136 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 1025 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.135 days = 4 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_core_of = ARM }
			remove_core_of = ARM
			if = {
				limit = { state = 353 }
				354 = { remove_claim_by = ARM }
				1034 = { remove_claim_by = ARM }
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_armenian_minority
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_attrition_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian = -0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian
			min = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_army_defence_factor_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_enemy_local_supplies_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian = -0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_recruitable_population_armenian_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian
			max = 0
		}
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level = -1 }
}

TUR_reduce_greek_level = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level < 2 } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_factories_greek = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_local_factories_greek
			max = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies_greek = -0.1 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies_greek
			min = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek
			max = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor_greek = -0.02 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor_greek
			min = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_core_of = GRE }
			remove_core_of = GRE
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_core_of = PON }
			remove_core_of = PON
			if = {
				limit = { state = 354 }
				1034 = { remove_claim_by = PON }
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_greek_minority
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_local_factories_greek_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_factories_greek = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_local_factories_greek
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_local_intel_to_enemies_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies_greek = -0.1 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies_greek
			min = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_recruitable_population_greek_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_local_construction_speed_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor_greek = -0.02 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek
			max = 0
		}
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level = -1 }
}

TUR_increase_christian_conscriptions_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
			check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek < 0 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_TUR_greek_minority_tt
		add_to_variable = {
			tooltip = recruitable_population_factor_5
			TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_south_slavic_minority }
			check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_south_slavic < 0 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_TUR_south_slavic_minority_tt
		add_to_variable = {
			tooltip = recruitable_population_factor_5
			TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_south_slavic = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
			check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian < 0 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_TUR_armenian_minority_tt
		add_to_variable = {
			tooltip = recruitable_population_factor_5
			TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_assyrian_minority }
			check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_assyrian < 0 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_TUR_assyrian_minority_tt
		add_to_variable = {
			tooltip = recruitable_population_factor_5
			TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_assyrian = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
			check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_georgian < 0 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_TUR_georgian_minority_tt
		add_to_variable = {
			tooltip = recruitable_population_factor_5
			TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_georgian = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
			check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_arab < 0 }

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
	}
}

			}
			if = {

				multiply_variable = { TUR_arab_population_political_power_factor = 5 }
			}
		}

			limit = {

								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_population_political_power_factor = 0 } }
							}

					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_arab_population_stability_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_arab_population_war_support_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_arab_population_political_power_factor = 0 }

		every_state = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_jewish_minority } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_variable = ROOT.TUR_jewish_population_factor }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_variable = ROOT.TUR_judaic_population_factor }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_variable = TUR_jewish_judaic_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_variable = TUR_jewish_judaic_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { controller = { has_idea = TUR_avraam_benaroya } }
				add_to_variable = { TUR_jewish_variable = 0.005 }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_variable = TUR_jewish_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_variable = 5 }
			set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = TUR_jewish_variable }
			set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = TUR_jewish_variable }
			#set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_political_power_factor = TUR_jewish_variable }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_political_power_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_political_power_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_jewish_population_political_power_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_ottoman_syria } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_political_power_factor = 3 }
			}
            if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ALB } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_political_power_factor = 5 }
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_jewish_minority } }
							NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_state_level > 0 } }
						}
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
							}
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
							}
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_jewish_population_political_power_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_political_power_factor = 0 } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_political_power_factor = 0 }
		}
		345 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_345_jewish_population_stability_factor = TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor } }
		347 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_347_jewish_population_stability_factor = TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor } }

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_kurdish_sunni_variable = ROOT.TUR_shia_population_factor }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_kurdish_sunni_variable = TUR_kurdish_sunni_state_level }

				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_kurdish_variable = TUR_kurdish_sunni_variable }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_kurdish_variable = TUR_kurdish_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_kurdish_variable = 5 }
			set_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_stability_factor = TUR_kurdish_variable }
			set_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_war_support_factor = TUR_kurdish_variable }
			#set_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_political_power_factor = TUR_kurdish_variable }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_stability_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_kurdish_population_stability_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_war_support_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }

				}

				multiply_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_political_power_factor = 5 }
			}

			limit = { 457 = { TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_committee_government = yes } }
			add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_aswan_political_power_factor = ROOT.TUR_457_state_political_power_factor }

		}
		set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_trablusgarp_political_power_factor = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { 448 = { TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_committee_government = yes } }

		}
		set_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_stability = 0 }
		every_state = {
			if = {
				limit = { TUR_state_has_minority_mtth = yes }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = THIS.TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = THIS.TUR_greek_population_stability_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = THIS.TUR_arab_population_stability_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = THIS.TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = THIS.TUR_south_slavic_population_stability_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = THIS.TUR_albanian_population_stability_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = THIS.TUR_kurdish_population_stability_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = THIS.TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = THIS.TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = THIS.TUR_turkish_population_stability_factor }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { TUR_state_has_autonomy_lebanon_mtth = yes }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = ROOT.TUR_ottoman_autonomy_lebanon_factor }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { TUR_state_has_autonomy_mtth = yes }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = ROOT.TUR_ottoman_autonomy_factor }

			if = {
				limit = { TUR_state_has_semi_autonomy_mtth = yes }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_stability = ROOT.TUR_ottoman_semi_autonomy_factor }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = 0 }
		every_state = {
			if = {
				limit = { TUR_state_has_minority_mtth = yes }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_arab_population_war_support_factor }

				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_south_slavic_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_albanian_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_kurdish_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor }

				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_turkish_population_war_support_factor }

			}

				limit = { TUR_state_has_autonomy_mtth = yes }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = ROOT.TUR_ottoman_autonomy_factor }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { TUR_state_has_semi_autonomy_mtth = yes }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = ROOT.TUR_ottoman_semi_autonomy_factor }
			}
		}
		#mecca resistance value
		670 = { set_variable = { global.TUR_mecca_resistance_target = TUR_ottoman_resistance_target_arab } }
		add_to_variable = { global.TUR_mecca_resistance_target = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { global.TUR_mecca_resistance_target_opposite = global.TUR_mecca_resistance_target }
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
		set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_tt = TUR_armenian_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_greek_population_tt = TUR_greek_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_tt = TUR_jewish_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_arab_population_tt = TUR_arab_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_tt = TUR_south_slavic_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_tt = TUR_albanian_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_tt = TUR_kurdish_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_tt = TUR_assyrian_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_tt = TUR_georgian_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_turkish_population_tt = TUR_turkish_population_factor }

		set_variable = { TUR_sunni_population_tt = TUR_sunni_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_orthodox_population_tt = TUR_orthodox_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_apostolic_population_tt = TUR_apostolic_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_judaic_population_tt = TUR_judaic_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_syriac_population_tt = TUR_syriac_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_shia_population_tt = TUR_shia_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_catholic_population_tt = TUR_catholic_population_factor }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_ottoman_syria }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_greek_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_arab_population_tt = 3 }

			multiply_variable = { TUR_sunni_population_tt = 3 }

			multiply_variable = { TUR_apostolic_population_tt = 3 }

			multiply_variable = { TUR_syriac_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_shia_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_catholic_population_tt = 3 }
		}
